6/20/22, 9:04 PM - 7: *We know most of you already had the word in mind, out of curiosity though what did you think when it first struck you?*

*Often times when we come across the word shifting paradigms we tend to think of something big, it almost feels like one of those 'my whole life is a lie' moments, for instance when we discovered that the Earth isn't flat.*

*You could even think of shifting paradigms as a Eureka moment when Newton explained gravity and Einstein introduced us to the concept of relativity.*

*Shifting paradigms was originally explained for the scientific theory but even the term had its shift as it gained popularity amongst other fields such as the paradigm shift created by Shakespeare's impact on drama and when jazz and rock revolutionised music.*

*We witnessed shifting paradigms in business with the emergence of e-commerce and Ed-tech during covid that took the market by storm.*

*And here at E-cell, we hope to be at the pinnacle of such shifting paradigms.*

Yes, it is Vignaharta- *ğŸ’«Lord GaneshağŸ’«*. In respect and devotion  to Ganesha, we celebrate Ganesh Chaturthi every year. With this year's Ganesh Chaturthi closing inâ³ï¸, *Bengaluru Ganesh Utsava* is organising a *"Clay Seed Ganesha Making"* event along with KSPCB and Rotary on August 28th, 2022 at National College Ground, Basavanagudi. About 10,000 participants are expected to take part. 

For this, volunteers are needed who can help with table arrangements, helping the participants, providing clay, etc. Volunteers are needed from 8am to 5:30pm. 

NOTE -  *T-shirts, Certificates, Breakfast, Lunch, Snacks*  will be provided to all volunteers by BGU. 
Also, *3 activity pointsğŸ¤©* will be provided to RVCE students 

While Ganesh Chaturthi is celebrated auspiciously, it has its own problems. Water pollution due to POP statues and toxic paint is one major problem which can be prevented by keeping Clay Ganesha. With this idea, let's all help BGU with the "Clay Seed Ganesha Making Event" by stepping up to volunteer and help celebrate a *pollution-free and greenğŸŒ±* Ganesh Chaturthi.

9/27/22, 1:42 PM - +91 80733 16197: The following are the points to be included in the DTL report as per the Principal.. (eventually it will go as a book/you all aware of it)
1.	Perspectives and building blocks
2.	Technology and systems
3.	Optimization and soft computing models
4.	Emerging trends in ----------
5.	Case studies (5 stages of DTL)

Suppose if the domain/cluster is Water conservation the above points will be viz.,
1.	Perspectives and building blocks: The perspective may be water availability, usage, distribution of water, per capita usage, etc
2.	Technology and systems: available water conservation technologies (literature survey) across the globe and related information
3.	 Optimizing the above sighted technologies: here the research gaps (Think global, act local approach)
4.	Emerging trends in the conservation of water
5.	All 5 phases of DTL
Sl. No. 1-4 will be common to all the students in a domain, distribute the work accordingly.
Sl. No. 5 is the individual DT work carried out, report it as a case study using all 5 stages of DTL.
Please show the report to Princy sir and finalize it.
The last date of the final report should be 29.09.2022. 
If any concerns we will discuss tomorrow in the regular DT class
